git svn clone svn+ssh://hakim@192.168.15.30/var/www/svn/dream/chubi/Trunk/Project ./ChubiGit

Art + Documentation: svn+ssh://hakim@192.168.15.30/var/www/svn/dream/chubi/Trunk/Documentation

to pull from svn:
git checkout master
git svn rebase # pull the commits from svn-server

then, to push all commits to svn:
git checkout develop # never use master branch for rebase's target!
git rebase master # replay all the commits on 'develop' into master
//git rebase master --committer-date-is-author-date # replay all the commits on 'develop' into master + keep the commit date
git svn dcommit # push everything to svn-server

in short to push to svn with selective commit
git checkout master
git svn rebase
#git checkout develop
#git rebase master --committer-date-is-author-date
git checkout -b pushing develop
git rebase -i master #then squash, delete, or unpick commits selectively
git svn dcommit
git checkout develop

delete all .svn folder recursively (rather than svn export)
find . -type d -name '.svn' -print -exec rm -rf {} \;

quickly revert everything back:
http://stackoverflow.com/questions/1146973/how-do-i-revert-all-local-changes-in-git-managed-project-to-previous-state
If you want to revert changes made to your working copy, do this:
git checkout .
If you want to revert changes made to the index (i.e., that you have added), do this:
git reset
If you want to revert a change that you have committed, do this:
git revert ...

"git checkout ." revert all unstaged changes, to the last checkout state
"git reset --hard" revert all changes (staged and unstaged), to the last checkout state
"git reset" merely unstage all staged changes

uncommit the last commit:
git reset --soft HEAD~1

delete all un-added files:
git clean -f

if you ever lost commit id or branch, use git reflog:
http://stackoverflow.com/a/135614/474330
The easiest way would be to find the head commit of the branch as it was immediately before the rebase started in the reflog...
"git reflog"
and to reset the current branch to it (with the usual caveats about being absolutely sure before reseting with the --hard option).
# Suppose the old commit was HEAD@{5} in the ref log
"git reset --hard HEAD@{5}"
You can check the history of the candidate old head by just doing a 
"git log HEAD@{5}"

git log filter all commits by root:
http://stackoverflow.com/a/20359396/474330
-. git config --global grep.patternType perl
-. git log --author='^((?!root).*)$'

git filter commits where a file was added: http://stackoverflow.com/a/13598028/474330
diff-filter: http://stackoverflow.com/a/6879568/474330
-. git log --diff-filter=A -- unity/main/Build/Worktionary.txt // added
-. git log --diff-filter=M -- *.txt // modified

git search commit-id by commit message:
-. git log --grep=commit_msgs_regex

git search commit-id by subversion number: e.g: search for R.20713
-. git log --grep=20713

figure out files changed between two commits:
git diff --name-only SHA1 SHA2 | grep .unity
git diff --name-only SHA1 SHA2
git diff --name-only HEAD~10 HEAD~5

figure out who write a particular function in what revision:
e.g: find UpdateJetDamage function with the diff
git log -S UpdateJetDamage --source --all -p
e.g: find UpdateJetDamage function
git log -S UpdateJetDamage --source --all

Show all changed file names between two different commits:
http://stackoverflow.com/a/1552353/474330
git diff --name-only SHA1 SHA2
git diff --name-only HEAD~10 HEAD~5 // to see the differences between the tenth latest commit and the fifth latest (or so).

git remove a specific (middle) commit with rebase:
http://stackoverflow.com/a/13389977/474330
Let's say you want to remove commit id: 4d19b3d
git rebase --onto 4d19b3d^ 4d19b3d

create patch for all commits since 918cd15 up to latest commit (sorted from 918cd15 to current)
http://stackoverflow.com/a/1892773/474330
git format-patch 918cd15 --stdout > diff.patch

git svn skip bogus commit revision
let's say the problematic revision is R.4535, and our latest "git svn log" is in R.4535 and there is an error:
Checksum mismatch: trunk/project/unity/main/Assets/main.sln 95c7ea059999e600e07a0d41f24c17e9b963807c
expected: 7ef381e06723b5dc76a236a88974f0fc
     got: 4deb9678c5db75a50c80ce44115ca68e
do: 
git svn fetch --ignore-paths='trunk/' -r4535:4536
afterwards, to resume, do:
git svn fetch

git checkout .
git clean -fd #remove all local modifications

#git rename tag
#http://stackoverflow.com/questions/1028649/how-do-you-rename-a-git-tag
#git tag new old
#git tag -d old
#git push origin :refs/tags/old
git tag push/2015/01/19 push/150119
git tag -d push/150119						# delete local tag
git push origin :push/150119				# delete remote tag. Important so that tag doesn't reappear on next fetch

pushing to git bare without checkout:
git svn fetch
git push origin --all

generate daily-delta for 26th February 2015:
git log --after="2015-02-25" --author=hakim > yandhie.txt
cat ./yandhie.txt | pbcopy

Couchbase server:
To remove:
remove databases on /Development/couchbase
remove Application Support on ~/Library/Application Support/Couchbase

Install:
couchbase-server-community_2.2.0_x86_64
run and choose Open Admin Console
setup and choose database path and indices path (both should point to the same folder)
Server hostname should be default: 127.0.0.1
choose start a new cluster and specify your ram quota (1024 - 2048 is recommended)
Create default bucket (no way to skip it)
specify admin username and password
wait 'til server is up
go to "Data Buckets"
delete of the "default" bucket
Create new data bucket, specify "Game" as bucket name and "Couchbase" as bucket type, 256 MB RAM, Access control Standard Port, NO replica, everything else default
Create new data bucket, specify "Session" as bucket name and "Memcached" as bucket type, 256 MB RAM, Access control Dedicated Port: 11212
Open /SvnProjRoot/Server/Server.sln with Xamarin, and Run Debug
Open unity, change connection settings to Local and run

list all server nodes:
http://127.0.0.1:8080/Chubi/Metadata

==========================================
= Communication infrastructure research: =
==========================================
Google:
Nearby Connections API
-. gotta join the same wifi network

Nearby Messages API
-. uses bluetooth and internet to relay messages
-. force turn on bluetooth on android even without declaring bluetooth permission

Apple:
Bonjour
-. classic bluetooth via input and output stream

Multipeer Connectivity
-. uses classic bluetooth, wifi infrastructure and ac-hoc/peer to peer wifi to send data
-. data sent as messages, stream or as resource

Android Plugin
[27/8/15 12:03:47 pm] Weiyi: Android Library projects should be added as a subdirectory in Assets/Plugins/Android, for example Assets/Plugins/Android/myandroidlibrary. It must contain project.properties file with android.library set to true, and AndroidManifest.xml - in that case it is recognized as an Android Library.

Then goes the manifest merging logic.
If you have your own manifest here: Assets/Plugins/Android/AndroidManifest.xml, it is taken as the base one, otherwise Unity default manifest is used as the base one.

Next, it gets merged with all Android Libraries' manifests.

Last step - properties, uses-features and permissions are set.

Hope that helps. (I would probably need to write a blog post on this topic).
[27/8/15 12:04:13 pm] Weiyi: from here http://forum.unity3d.com/threads/obsolete-providing-android-resources-in-assets-plugins-android-res-is-deprecated.315889/

troubleshooting:

how to debug as other user from unity editor:
1. get the player's user name from Settings, eg: d2fba444-3c59-4022-ba1f-e7ff87ddc3a6
2. go to couchbase and get the player summary document, eg: http://127.0.0.1:8091/index.html#sec=documents&bucketName=Game&documentsPageNumber=0&docId=s_player_d2fba444-3c59-4022-ba1f-e7ff87ddc3a6
3. get the user id from player summary document, eg: http://127.0.0.1:8091/index.html#sec=documents&bucketName=Game&documentsPageNumber=0&docId=user_f977e5e5-386b-4014-b77a-0da79567bcf3
4. you can find the Username from the user_xxx document, put it in Connection.cs > Initialize() and you are good to go, eg: Username = "z7cBqjQ7b3RM3TxACn4oHKoOyQA=";

git grep from log: http://stackoverflow.com/a/7125014/474330
Put this in ~/.gitconfig:

[alias]
    find = log --pretty=\"format:%Cgreen%H %Cblue%s\" --name-status --grep

Then type "git find string" to get a list of all the commits containing that string in the message.

150209:
// 3 players:
// CA attack, S stay still, CB stay still
// CB enemy die first, followed by S, then CA, both clients reflect same health
// S attack, CA stay still, CB stay still, both clients enemy die first at the same time

if ( MultiplayerManager.Instance.CurrentPlayer.MultiplayerRole != NetworkPlayer.EMULTIPLAYER_ROLE.EMR_SERVER ) {
	if ( iCurrentHealth != ((int)pVictim.Health) && pVictim.Health > iCurrentHealth ) {
		float fOffsetDamage = pVictim.Health - iCurrentHealth;
		pVictim.InflictDamage( pAttacker, (StageCharacter)null, fOffsetDamage, Vector3.zero, true, false );
	}
}

150206:
Optimizing iOS BluetoothLE
* A characteristic contains a SINGLE value that represents more information about a peripheral’s service. For example, a temperature measurement characteristic of a health thermometer service may have a value that indicates a temperature in Celsius. You can retrieve the value of a characteristic by reading it directly or by subscribing to it.

141125:
adb install for all devices:
for SERIAL in $(adb devices | grep -v List | cut -f 1);
do 
echo "Installing to $SERIAL"
`adb -s $SERIAL shell pm list packages -f | grep rocket`
`adb -s $SERIAL install -r testbuild.apk`;
`adb -s $SERIAL shell pm list packages -f | grep rocket`
done

uninstall and restart all devices:
for SERIAL in $(adb devices | grep -v List | cut -f 1); do `adb -s $SERIAL uninstall sg.dreamrocket.chubi`; `adb -s $SERIAL reboot`; done

adb -s BX903HJP8T logcat | grep `adb -s BX903HJP8T shell ps | grep sg.dreamrocket.chubi | cut -c10-15` > BX903HJP8T.txt
adb -s 001947d03f58ce logcat | grep `adb -s 001947d03f58ce shell ps | grep sg.dreamrocket.chubi | cut -c10-15` > 001947d03f58ce.txt

delegate void btcallback();
private Bluetooth bluetoothDeviceScript = null;
private List<string> connectedDevices = new List<string>();
private List<string> subscribedCharacteristics = new List<string>();

private static BtManager s_cBtManager = null;
public static BtManager Instance { get { return s_cBtManager; } private set { s_cBtManager = value; } }
	
	public static string uuidService = "00001454-0000-1000-8000-00805f9b34fb";
	public static string uuidCharacteristic = "00002afa-0000-1000-8000-00805f9b34fb";
	
	private ECONNECTION_STATE ecsCurrent;
	private ECONNECTION_STATE ecsInit;
	
	public Action<string>		onEventDeviceConnected;
	public Action<string>		onEventDeviceDisconnected;
	public Action<string>		onEventDataSent;
	public Action<byte[]>		onEventDataReceived;
	
	private byte[] data = new byte[1024];
	private bool dataDirty;
	
	public bool IsLE()

	void OnConnected(string deviceId)				// callback to onEventDeviceConnected
	void OnDisconnected(string deviceId)			// callback to onEventDeviceDisconnected

	public void OnCentralSent(string deviceId)		// callback to onEventDataSent
	public void OnPeripheralSent(string deviceId)	// callback to onEventDataSent
	
	void OnCentralReceive(byte[] byData)			// callback to onEventDataReceived
	void OnPeripheralReceive(byte[] byData)			// callback to onEventDataReceived

	void StartCentral()	
	void StartPeripheral()
	
/**
 * 	note: called when subscribed data was changed + broadcasted by peripheral
 */
void peripheralDidUpdateValueForCharacteristic(byte[] byData)	// callback to onEventDataReceived
/**
 * note: key
 */
void PeripheralDidReceiveData(byte[] byData)		// callback to onEventDataReceived
void OnDisconnection(string device)					// callback to onEventDeviceDisconnected

void CreatePeripheralCharacteristic(btcallback callback, string name)
void CentralDiscoveredCharacteristic(string name, string serviceId, string characteristicId)
void CentralDiscoveredPeripheral(string device, string name)

void SubscriptionFromCentral(string characteristicId, string centralId)		// note: todo: - we cannot stop advertising once there is one central connected to us

BtManager

public static string uuidService = "00001454-0000-1000-8000-00805f9b34fb";
public static string uuidCharacteristic = "00002afa-0000-1000-8000-00805f9b34fb";

	private ECONNECTION_STATE ecsCurrent;
	private ECONNECTION_STATE ecsInit;

	public Action<string>		onEventDeviceConnected;
	public Action<string>		onEventDeviceDisconnected;
	public Action<string>		onEventDataSent;
	public Action<byte[]>		onEventDataReceived;

	private byte[] data = new byte[1024];
	private bool dataDirty;

	private List<string> connectedDevices;

	public bool IsLE()
	
	void OnConnected(string deviceId)	// callback to onEventDeviceConnected
	
	void OnDisconnected(string deviceId)	// callback to onEventDeviceDisconnected

	void UpdatePeripheral()	// may send data if connected as peripheral / server and data is dirty
	
	void UpdateCentral()	// may send data if connected as central / client and data is dirty

	void OnCentralSent(string deviceId)	// callback to onEventDataSent

	void OnCentralReceive(byte[] byData)	// callback to onEventDataReceived

	void OnPeripheralSent(string deviceId)	// callback to onEventDataSent
	
	void OnPeripheralReceive(byte[] byData)	// callback to onEventDataReceived

150413 cutting down comm, shared client send to server and server broadcast to all:
	public void SendActReadyToShop( bool bReady ) {
		UniversalLogger.LogInfo("[MultiplayerManager] SendActReadyToShop : " + bReady);

		NetworkPlayer pServer = getNetworkPlayerConnectedServer();

		byte[] pbySent = CurrentPlayer.sendAllLobbyReadyToShop( pServer.PlayerId, CurrentPlayer.PlayerId, bReady );
		if ( CurrentPlayer.MultiplayerRole == NetworkPlayer.EMULTIPLAYER_ROLE.EMR_SERVER ) {
			receiveAllLobbyReadyToShop( CurrentPlayer.PlayerId, pbySent );
		}
	}
	
	public byte[] sendAllLobbyReadyToShop(string szServerId, string szPlayerId, bool bReady)
	{
		UniversalLogger.LogInfo("[NetworkPlayer] sendAllLobbyReadyToShop : " + szServerId);

		byte[] pbyMessage = new byte[BtStreamHelper.BUFFER_SIZE];

		byte byCommand = (byte)MultiplayerManager.EMESSAGE_SEQUENCE.EMB_LOBBY_CA_READY_TO_SHOP;
		byte[] pbyPlayerId = BtStreamHelper.PackString(szPlayerId);
		byte byValue = bReady ? (byte)1 : (byte)0;

		int iIndex = 0;
		pbyMessage[iIndex++] = byCommand;
		BtStreamHelper.WriteBytes( ref pbyMessage, ref iIndex, pbyPlayerId );
		pbyMessage[iIndex++] = byValue;

		if ( MultiplayerRole == EMULTIPLAYER_ROLE.EMR_CLIENT ) {
			// I am client, so I send to the server
			BtManager.Instance.DataSendToSpecific( szServerId, pbyMessage, true );
		} else {
			// I am server, so I broadcast to everyone
			BtManager.Instance.DataBroadcastToAll( pbyMessage, true );
		}
		return pbyMessage;
	}
	
	private void receiveAllLobbyReadyToShop(string szSenderId, byte[] byMessage)
	{
		UniversalLogger.LogInfo("[MultiplayerManager] receiveAllLobbyReadyToShop SENDER: " + szSenderId);

		int iIndex = 1;
		string szPlayerId = BtStreamHelper.ReadString( byMessage, ref iIndex );
		byte byReady = byMessage[iIndex++];

		if ( CurrentPlayer.MultiplayerRole == NetworkPlayer.EMULTIPLAYER_ROLE.EMR_SERVER ) {
			// I am server, if I received from other people, I need to forward to all
			if ( !CurrentPlayer.PlayerId.Equals(szPlayerId) ) {
				CurrentPlayer.sendAllLobbyReadyToShop( CurrentPlayer.PlayerId, szPlayerId, byReady == 1 );
			}
		} else {
			// I am client, I just need to consume
		}

		NetworkPlayer pPlayer = getNetworkPlayerByDeviceId (szPlayerId, LobbyPlayers);
		if ( pPlayer == null ) {
			return;
		}
		if ( byReady == 0 ) {
			pPlayer.CurrentGameState = NetworkPlayer.EMULTIPLAYER_GAMESTATE.EMGS_LOBBY;
		} else {
			pPlayer.CurrentGameState = NetworkPlayer.EMULTIPLAYER_GAMESTATE.EMGS_READYTOSHOP;
		}

		if ( onLobbyEventReadyToShop != null ) {
			onLobbyEventReadyToShop( pPlayer, byReady == 1 );
		}
	}
	
	
	
	
	public string sendSpecificIngamePlayerDie( string szToServer )
	{
		string szMessage = MultiplayerManager.MessageSequence [(int)MultiplayerManager.EMESSAGE_SEQUENCE.EMS_INGAME_CS_PLAYER_DIE];
		BtManager.Instance.DataSendToSpecific( szToServer, MultiplayerManager.GetBytes( szMessage ), false );
		return szMessage;
	}

	public string sendBroadcastIngamePlayerDie( string szDeadPlayerId )
	{
		StringBuilder sbMessage = new StringBuilder(MultiplayerManager.MessageSequence[(int)MultiplayerManager.EMESSAGE_SEQUENCE.EMS_INGAME_SA_PLAYER_DIE]);
		sbMessage.Append("~");
		sbMessage.Append(szDeadPlayerId);
		BtManager.Instance.DataBroadcastToAll( MultiplayerManager.GetBytes( sbMessage.ToString() ), false );
		return sbMessage.ToString();
	}
	
	private void receiveSpecificIngamePlayerDie( string szSenderId, string szMessage )
	{
		UniversalLogger.LogInfo("[MultiplayerManager] receiveSpecificIngamePlayerDie: " + szSenderId + ", " + szMessage);
//		NetworkPlayer pSender = getNetworkPlayerByDeviceId( szSenderId, GamePlayers );
//		if ( pSender != null ) {
//			pSender.CurrentGameState = NetworkPlayer.EMULTIPLAYER_GAMESTATE.EMGS_INGAME_DIE;
//		}
		UniversalLogger.LogInfo("[MultiplayerManager] receiveSpecificIngamePlayerDie: " + szSenderId + " IS DEAD!");

		if ( CurrentPlayer.MultiplayerRole == NetworkPlayer.EMULTIPLAYER_ROLE.EMR_SERVER ) {
			string szBroadcast = CurrentPlayer.sendBroadcastIngamePlayerDie( szSenderId );
			receiveBroadcastIngamePlayerDie( CurrentPlayer.PlayerId, szBroadcast );
		}
	}	
	
	private void receiveBroadcastIngamePlayerDie( string szSenderId, string szMessage )
	{
		UniversalLogger.LogInfo("[MultiplayerManager] receiveBroadcastIngamePlayerDie: " + szSenderId + ", " + szMessage);
		string[] parts = MultiplayerManager.SplitString( szMessage );

		// parts[0] = EMSI_
		// parts[1] = dead player's id
		if ( parts.Length < 2 ) {
			// invalid message
			UniversalLogger.LogError("[MultiplayerManager] receiveBroadcastIngamePlayerDie ERROR INVALID MESSAGE " + szMessage);
			return;
		}

		NetworkPlayer pPlayerDie = getNetworkPlayerByDeviceId( parts[1], GamePlayers );
		UniversalLogger.LogInfo("[MultiplayerManager] receiveBroadcastIngamePlayerDie: PRE PLAYER: " + pPlayerDie);
		if ( !pPlayerDie.IsDead() && pPlayerDie.WaitCollect == false ) { // TODO: player recovered but not yet collected (BlocksToHeal == 0), shouldnt go inside here
			// not dead yet, indicate that player is dead
			pPlayerDie.BlocksToHeal = NetworkPlayer.MaxBlocksToHeal;
			if ( onGameEventPlayerDie != null ) {
				onGameEventPlayerDie( pPlayerDie );
			}
		}
		if ( CurrentPlayer.MultiplayerRole == NetworkPlayer.EMULTIPLAYER_ROLE.EMR_SERVER ) {
			bool bAllDead = GamePlayers.TrueForAll( pPlayer => {
				return pPlayer.IsDead();
			});
			if ( bAllDead ) {
				string szBroadcast = CurrentPlayer.sendBroadcastIngameGameBacktoworld();
				receiveBroadcastIngameGameBacktoworld( CurrentPlayer.PlayerId, szBroadcast );
			}
		}
		UniversalLogger.LogInfo("[MultiplayerManager] receiveBroadcastIngamePlayerDie: POST PLAYER: " + pPlayerDie);
	}

{0} started the game

4. MSG_GEN_MULTIPLAY_START_TIME_TXT
The Game will start in {0}s
{0}: Time (in secs) to countdown for Players who are ready

5. MSG_GEN_MULTIPLAY_KICK_TIME_TXT
You will be kicked out of Group in {0}s
{0}: Time (in secs) to countdown for Player who is not ready

6. MSG_GEN_MULTIPLAY_CHANGE_CHAR
{0} switched to another Character
{0}: FB Name if logged in to FB, else Char Base Name of Host, MSG_GEN_YOU_TXT (if you are the Player doing the change)

stability improvement during scanning:

iOS
-. upgrade to iOS 8.3 doesn't eliminate the connection and discovery problem on the iPad Mini (device id: iOS6), however, stability does improve and consistently able to search and connect
-. discovery problem was due to the host. Even though startAdvertising executes as usual with no indicator of problem at all, no device are able to find it at all. This problem is isolated to only host.. if the same device is immediately switched to client mode, it can read all the available host and connect to them successfully. This problem can be eliminated by switching bluetooth off and on again, but Apple do not expose any public API for switching bluetooth on/off
-. turning bluetooth off and on seems to solve the discoverability issue for the host. (host need to restart to be found)

Android
1. Android-5 redmi phone cannot be guest, but can be host
2. Android-1 S2 phone can be both, but bluetooth module may be problematic and cause device to auto-restart continuously until hard-resetted
3. Unlabelled Xperia phone has no bluetooth connectivity problem
4. switch to secured authenticated rfcomm socket, which requires pairing, but is more reliable

sendBroadcastLobbyGamePlayerDetail(int iIndex, int iTotalPlayers, int iConnectionState, int iConfirmationId, string szPlayerId, string szBroadcastData)

			int iConnectionState = System.Convert.ToInt32(parts[3]);
			int iConfirmationId = System.Convert.ToInt32(parts[4]);
			string szPlayerId = parts[5];
			NetworkPlayer pPlayer = getNetworkPlayerByDeviceId(szPlayerId, GamePlayers);
			UniversalLogger.LogInfo("[MultiplayerManager] receiveBroadcastLobbyGamePlayerDetail PRE: " + pPlayer);
			if ( pPlayer != null ) {
				BtDevice pDevice = pPlayer.Device;
				if ( pDevice == null ) {
					StringBuilder sbBroadcastData = new StringBuilder(parts[6]);
					for ( int i = 7; i < parts.Length; i++ ) {
						sbBroadcastData.Append("~");
						sbBroadcastData.Append(parts[i]);
					}
					pDevice = BtManager.Instance.createDevice(szPlayerId, (BtManager.ECONNECTION_STATE)iConnectionState, MultiplayerManager.GetBytes(sbBroadcastData.ToString()));
					pPlayer.Device = pDevice;
				} else {
					UniversalLogger.LogInfo("[MultiplayerManager] receiveBroadcastLobbyGamePlayerDetail DEVICE: " + pPlayer);
				}
				if ( pPlayer.ConfirmationId != iConfirmationId ) {
					UniversalLogger.LogInfo("[MultiplayerManager] receiveBroadcastLobbyGamePlayerDetail ERROR INCORRECT ConfirmationId : " + pPlayer.ConfirmationId + " != " + iConfirmationId);
				}
				pPlayer.ConfirmPlayer( iConfirmationId );
			} else {
				UniversalLogger.LogInfo("[MultiplayerManager] receiveBroadcastLobbyGamePlayerDetail ERROR PLAYER IS NULL!");
			}
			UniversalLogger.LogInfo("[MultiplayerManager] receiveBroadcastLobbyGamePlayerDetail POST: " + pPlayer);
